Well, 
I am not sure what I did because I closed cmd.

But I ran:
$ pluto build
$ pluto fetch

and now I can see an additional HTML file in the root that shows the "top" 
template view.

[image: topsnip.png]


It is working locally and this is pretty awesome! Amazing how a couple 
lines of code can deploy a webpage!
